Country Subdivision (ISO 3166-2)	PHVS_CountrySubdivision_ISO_3166-2	2.16.840.1.114222.4.11.3286	1	ISO 3166-2:Codes for the representation of names of countries and their subdivisions - Part 2: Country subdivision code which gives codes for the names of the principal subdivisions (e.g provinces or states) of all countries coded in ISO 3166-1. This code is based on the two-letter code element from ISO 3166-1 followed by a separator and a further string of up to three alphanumeric characters. Keywords: IS0 3166-2 Part 2, Country subdivision, Country Subdivisions, Provinces	Published	03/16/2010	Country Subdivision (ISO 3166-2)
